Petition from Overseas Chinese Female Students to the Chinese Red Cross Society 158

The Overseas Chinese Relief Committee of Soetong, Dutch East Indies, sent a letter to the Chinese Red Cross Society, which stated: "Respected Sirs, we hereby inform you that six female overseas Chinese students from Medan, Lin Qionghua, Lin Yuyao, Chen Yueqing, Yan Chun'e, Wen Taoqing, and Peng Baoying, have written to us stating that they wish to gather six like-minded comrades, with the permission of their parents, to join the Shanghai Chinese Red Cross Society and learn first aid. They hope to contribute their meager efforts in the future and fulfill their duty to the nation. They request your esteemed society to provide a letter of introduction and detailed instructions on the procedures for joining and learning, so that they can comply. We have verified that Lin Qionghua and the other five students are all overseas Chinese students from Sumatra, graduates of either Chinese middle schools or Dutch-Chinese schools. They are of upright character and sound health. This time, they are determined to return to the country and enthusiastically assist in disaster relief, with the consent of their parents. Our committee believes that charitable work is the highest expression of human emotion and should grant their request to encourage them. We have always known that your esteemed society has a grand scale and a pure mission. These enthusiastic overseas Chinese female students have come from afar and should be appreciated by your esteemed society. However, our committee has not been informed of the detailed procedures for joining and learning, and we cannot convey them. Therefore, we respectfully send this letter for inquiry and request a reply." After receiving this letter, the Society sent the regulations of the nursing school and approved the request.

Red Swastika Society Buries Corpses in Nanxiang and Other Places 159

The East Asia Relief Team of the World Red Swastika Society, after receiving a telegram from the 19th Route Army requesting the team to bury the corpses in the Huangdu, Nanxiang, and Jiading areas, specially dispatched team members Ge Zhicheng, Yin Zhenzi, Han Luchong, Ouyang Guanjun, and others, leading ten laborers, and carrying burial tools. They departed from Suzhou on the 18th of last month and arrived in Kunshan. After contacting the 19th Route Army for arrangements, they took a car to Nanxiang. On the 19th, they began work, burying seven corpses in the wheat fields west of Nanxiang Railway Station. They also buried three corpses next to the Yijia Temple, four miles from Nanxiang, and four corpses at Yuanmian Bridge. At 5 PM, they went to places outside the east gate of Jiading and buried a total of thirteen corpses that had been bombed. They also buried one exposed corpse in an open space about two miles from the city, and two exposed corpses in a wheat field about two miles outside the north gate. Furthermore, in the wasteland, they collected and buried many scattered corpses and bone fragments, too numerous to count. On the 21st, they departed for Tangzhen and the surrounding areas, burying a total of twenty-one exposed corpses. There was a rotting corpse in a pond, which they immediately retrieved and buried. They also buried twelve exposed corpses at Shuangshi Bridge, five miles from the town, and one corpse in the grassland to the west. On the 22nd, they buried three exposed corpses in various places in the east gate. On the 23rd, they returned to Huangdu and buried nineteen corpses under Railway Bridge No. 24, west of the station. They then went north for about one mile to a river bend, where there was a rotting corpse. Unable to retrieve it, they buried it on the riverbank with a thick layer of soil. Next to the Yangshu Tomb, two miles from the station, they buried one exposed corpse. At 5:30 PM, they returned to Suzhou from Huangdu by car. This trip lasted six days, during which they buried a total of ninety-six corpses. The corpses in various places had been exposed for a long time, gnawed by dogs and eaten by eagles. The stench was overwhelming, and most of the bodies were incomplete, with exposed organs or gouged eyes and noses. The various tragic scenes were unbearable to witness. Alas, how tragic!

Muslims Arrive in Shanghai from Arabia 160

Fifty Muslims, clients of Shanghai, set sail from Shanghai for Jeddah. The China Travel Service on Sichuan Road in Shanghai was responsible for handling their travel arrangements and providing all services, ensuring their convenience and comfort along the way. The group arrived in Shanghai on the 29th of last month aboard the Blue Funnel Line's Aclielles. The travel agency had also negotiated with the shipping company to provide a special small steamship to transport the Muslims and their luggage from the Pudong Wharf to the Xinguang Wharf for disembarkation and then to the Ximen Church. The group expressed their exceptional gratitude for the travel agency's thoughtful service.

Local Court Burns Confiscated Narcotics 161

The Shanghai Local Court incinerated narcotics confiscated in the first half of the 20th year of the Republic, including opium, opium paste, opium dross, opium ash, opium dross materials, opium water, heroin, morphine, red pills, white pills, black pills, and poisonous powder. The original sealed quantities included 7,936.2 taels and 544 catties of opium, 68.03 taels of opium paste plus eight small boxes, one small jar, and one small can, 6.93 taels of opium dross plus 239 pieces and three small boxes, 8.18 taels of opium ash, nine bottles of opium water, 61.302 catties of opium dross materials plus two small pieces, eight catties of opium leaves, one package of residue, nine catties plus 108.82 taels of heroin, 242 small boxes and 23.6 taels of morphine plus one small package, one small bottle of anesthetic, 1,704.5 taels and 214 boxes plus 5,124 pieces and 70 catties of red pills, 2.66 taels of red pill ash plus four iron boxes, 182 taels of red pill material, ten boxes of white pills, fourteen boxes of black pills, 81 taels of poisonous powder, and various drug paraphernalia. The matter was reported to the Jiangsu High Court, which designated May 31st for incineration and appointed Chief Clerk Yu Zongjian to supervise. The Ministry of Justice also sent Yang Zhaoxin and Chen Jingzhai to supervise. The court also invited representatives from various agencies to supervise the incineration. Yesterday, at 10 AM, the incineration took place. Representatives present included Song Yuntao from the Municipal Public Security Bureau, Ju Zhijing from the First Special Court, Zhang Wenbo from the Second Special Court, and Wang Zongjian from Customs. They were greeted by Court President Shen Xiqing, Chief Prosecutor Liu Maochu, and Duty Prosecutor Yang Qi and led to the seated area under the mat shed in the open space in front of the court prison. Then, Police Chief Xu Jinqing and Police Officers Chen Xihui and Chen Junfang supervised all the bailiffs and servants to unpack the opium one by one and weigh it in public. Then, they set it on fire with pine firewood, poured kerosene and salt, and ignited it. It was not completed until 3 PM. All the ashes were packed in hemp bags and sent by the police officers to the Huangpu River to be sunk to eliminate the toxic atmosphere.

Record of the Executive Supervisory Committee of the Lawyers Association 162

109th Meeting

Extension of Enrollment Deadline for Poor Education Fund 163

The Poor Education Fund has continued to operate as usual this year, despite the extremely unstable situation and social economic panic. The deadline for applying for subsidies for this year's enrollment was originally set for the end of May, but due to the later start of the new semester at various universities and the postal strike, the deadline has been extended to the end of June to increase coverage. The examination period is expected to be in early August. It is also heard that some students who have recently registered for the examination have attached registration fees, which is a misunderstanding. The committee has returned them separately, as the Fund Committee absolutely does not charge any fees to candidates.

Bandit Shoots and Wounds Head of Pujiang Zhangjialou Security Corps 164

Qu Baichun Bravely Wounded

Police Will Conduct Strict Inspections

On the evening of the 29th of last month, at about 7 PM, bandits suddenly arrived in batches in Zhangjialou Town, Pudong. Qu Baichun, the head of the Yangjing District Security Corps, followed the bandits with a gun to investigate. He was suddenly shot in a vital area by the bandits. He was sent to the hospital for treatment afterward. The findings of the investigation are recorded below:

Chasing Bandits and Being Shot On the evening of the 29th, at about 7 PM, many bandits suddenly came to the town, in twos and threes, forming teams from the west, looking around, and then returning east to west. There were about twenty of them. Qu Baichun, the owner of the Yongsheng Rice Shop in the town (who is also the head of the 22nd Ward and the head of the Security Corps), was keeping accounts when he saw this situation and became suspicious. He immediately secretly instructed all members of the town's Security Corps to be on high alert. Qu then carried a Mauser rifle and secretly investigated behind the bandit party. When he reached the center of the town, Qu questioned the bandits about where they were going. Unexpectedly, the bandits had already noticed. One of the bandits preemptively retreated two steps, took out a pistol from his sleeve, and fired four shots backwards. One shot hit Qu's chest. Mr. Qu remained extremely calm, lay on the ground, and fired seven or eight shots, hitting a bandit in a vital area, but he still escaped. Therefore, the bandit party's attempt to rob was unsuccessful. At that time, all members of the town's Security Corps fired their guns and searched in various directions. In the fields on the west side, they found a blood-stained twill white short shirt discarded by the wounded bandit, with two bullet holes in the back, one clean and one with hair, as if the bullet had entered from the left side and exited from the right side. There were also two felt hats, one gray and one dark red velvet, as well as a blue plaid wool long gown and a navy blue serge long gown.

Qu's Injuries After Qu was shot and injured, the Security Corps members were unaware of it until they heard his cries for help. When they went to investigate, they helped him up, but he was bleeding all over the ground. They managed to send him to the Sacred Heart Hospital on Ningguo Road in Yangshupu that night for treatment. Because the bullet was deeply embedded under his right rib, they obtained the consent of his family and Dr. Zhang Youmei and Dr. Ma Shijiong performed surgery to open his abdomen. They found that the bullet was deeply embedded inside the liver and difficult to remove. They temporarily sutured the wound in the liver, and if his condition worsened, they would perform a final operation to remove the bullet. According to the hospital's announcement, Mr. Qu's condition was as follows: At 8 AM on the 30th, his temperature was 38 degrees and his pulse was 96. He urinated once at 7 AM, 500 CC. At 4 PM on the 30th, his temperature was 39.3 degrees and his pulse was 112. At 8 AM on the 31st, his temperature was 37.8 degrees and his pulse was 96. He urinated twice and had no bowel movements. It is heard that his injuries are very critical. Yesterday, Xu Baoming, the head of the Yangjing District Security Corps, reported to his superiors for verification.

Who Is He? After the incident, the Security Corps members were on high alert all night. At dawn, they suddenly encountered a man in the east of the town who was lingering and unwilling to leave. When he saw people, he looked flustered and extremely suspicious. He was arrested and sent to the Second Branch of the Third District. According to his confession, his name is Bao Jinxian, he is from Shandong, and he lives in the eighteenth room on the east side of Qichang Inn. He is currently working in a yarn factory. Since there is no yarn factory in Zhangjialou, his confession was very contradictory. Yesterday, the director ordered him to be sent to the General Bureau for interrogation.

Unity and Security Zhangjialou is located southwest of Yangjing Town in Pudong, about six miles away from the Huangpu River, and is under the jurisdiction of the Second Branch of the Third District. There are dozens of shops open in the town. Most of the residents in the town are Catholics. Over time, the town has become an area for Catholic believers. These people are wealthy and have an unusually strong sense of unity. In the first year of the Republic, Qu Baichun (the head of the 26th Ward), the owner of the Yongsheng Rice Shop in the town, organized a commercial corps, raised funds to purchase firearms, and achieved excellent results. In the second year of the Republic, when Mr. Chen Ying'shi failed in the battle in Shanghai, a small number of soldiers fled to the town. Mr. Qu immediately set up machine guns at the main roads at the entrance of the town, sent personnel to guard them, and summoned the corps members to fire their guns to repel the soldiers. The soldiers were scattered, and the town was able to escape the danger. Later, the commercial corps was ordered to be reorganized into a Security Corps, and Mr. Qu was appointed as the head of the corps. Qu firmly declined, so the General Headquarters hired him as the head of the corps and divided the corps members into the First Team of the Yangjing District. The reason why the town has been peaceful to this day and the thieves have not dared to move is due to the strong unity of the residents.

Inspection and Prevention of Bandits Local merchants and residents believe that after the end of the Shanghai War, Zhabei, Jiangwan, Wusong, and Zhenru were taken over by our police. Most of the ruffians and traitors, knowing that they had nowhere to go, crossed the river to the east. Therefore, robbery cases have occurred frequently in Pudong recently. After the bandit shooting of the head of the Security Corps in Zhangjialou, they were very frightened and specially requested the police authorities to strictly inspect those with suspicious traces in the area near the Huangpu River to prevent the bandits from mixing in and to ensure safety. It is heard that the police authorities immediately ordered their subordinates to pay attention to prevention and strictly inspect.

Large Gambling Den Under Japanese Protection Raided 165

Qingshui Wensheng Sets Up a Scam

Ignorant Chinese Fall for the Trap

Police Arrest More Than Ten People

Negotiations Demanding Compensation

Since the Japanese forcibly occupied Zhabei, several months have passed. The Japanese have seen this as a rare opportunity to make money. Among them, there are various illegal matters such as promoting prostitution, sheltering opium, and openly gambling, all kinds of things. Moreover, many Japanese rogues have taken the opportunity to set up scams, fooling the Chinese into opening gambling venues, while they take advantage of them. The number of Chinese who have been harmed by them is countless. Yesterday, the Public Concession Police raided a gambling venue at the bottom of Wusong Road, Shenjiawan, which was a scene of Japanese rogues setting up a scam. It also involved a certain major general of the Japanese army. The details are recorded below:

The Dasheng Club Since the Japanese army occupied Zhabei on March 2nd, it was widely rumored that the Japanese would openly set up gambling venues in the forcibly occupied areas. At that time, the general public did not dare to believe it. Unexpectedly, within ten days, the rumor became a reality. More than ten gambling venues, large and small, were established at the same time. Later, after the agreement was reached, the Japanese army gradually withdrew, and unfortunately, the puppet traitors had internal strife. Therefore, in the most recent week, all the gambling venues closed down. The only one that survived was the Dasheng Club at No. 16 Shoudeli, Shenjiawan, at the bottom of Wusong Road. The reason why it stood alone was said to be backed by the Japanese rogue Qingshui Wensheng.

The Japanese Rogue Sets Up a Scam The Japanese rogue Qingshui Wensheng claimed to be one of Japan's writers. Who this person is, the Chinese are not clear about. Two weeks ago, Qingshui vigorously persuaded a certain Cantonese, saying that he and a certain major general currently stationed at the Zhabei Japanese Army Headquarters were classmates. Anything that anyone cannot do, he can handle it single-handedly. The Cantonese was moved by this and joined friends to raise funds to open the Dasheng Club at No. 16 Shoudeli, Shenjiawan, at the bottom of Wusong Road.

Detective's Raid When the Cantonese was negotiating with Qingshui, it was agreed that the Japanese Army Headquarters would issue a permit, and a fee of 250 yuan in Qing Dynasty currency would be paid every day, paid on a daily basis and not overdue or short. In addition, Qingshui would be given a reward of 3,000 yuan. After the negotiation was completed, the money was exchanged, and the so-called Headquarters permit was issued on the same day. A week ago, it began to operate. Unexpectedly, at about 5 PM yesterday, Liu Shaokui, a Chinese detective chief of the Public Concession Police, suddenly led Chinese and Western detectives to No. 16 Shoudeli. They arrested more than ten staff members and gamblers on the spot, and took all the gambling equipment and exhibits to the police station, waiting to be sent to court for investigation.

Demanding Compensation It is heard that among the more than ten people arrested, there were two Japanese. These two Japanese were said to have been recommended by Qingshui. Since the case occurred, the Cantonese was very angry, thinking that the Japanese Qingshui should not have set up a scam, causing such a major loss. The Cantonese intends to first seriously negotiate with Qingshui, demanding compensation. If there is no satisfactory reply, he will take photos of the issued permit and publish them in Chinese and Western newspapers to expose the conspiracy of the Japanese.

More Narcotics and Raw Materials Seized in the Japanese Morphine Manufacturing Case 166

Many Wooden Boxes and Parts

Police Take Photos for Detailed Study

Wang Changgen and Cao Bingkun, the Chinese detective chiefs of the Public Concession Police Headquarters, previously joined forces with Pan Gensi, the Western detective chief of the Narcotics Division, and Song Bingzheng, the Chinese detective, to raid a morphine manufacturing facility at No. 18 West Jiaxing Road. They arrested ten people, including the Japanese Nakamura and the Chinese Fang Yinbao, Lin Huiqing, and Zhou Yongyuan. They seized a large number of morphine drugs and machinery worth more than 35,000 yuan. The Japanese Nakamura was sent to the Japanese Consulate for interrogation, and Fang Yinbao and the other nine people were sent to the First Special Court for interrogation. These details have been reported in this newspaper. Yesterday morning, Judge Qiao Wanxuan presided over a further hearing at the High Court. Zhang Tianyin, the police lawyer, stated that during the adjournment, the Chinese and Western detectives who handled the case went to the site for further investigation. They searched and found four bottles of medicine, two yellow and two black. The yellow ones were opium dross, and the bottles were labeled in Japanese. The black ones were also opium materials. They also seized two account books, which stated that they were all for selling morphine for export. In addition, they found many wooden boxes in the house next door to No. 16. The format of the wooden boxes was the same as the wooden boxes seized at the original site. The house was also rented by a Japanese. These wooden boxes were prepared to pack and export the morphine after it was manufactured. The nine and a half pounds of white powder seized last time were chemically tested and found to be heroin, which is even more potent than morphine. Because there were so many various parts, the police took photos to keep them as evidence. Who rented the house has not yet been found out. The various drugs seized last time were initially chemically tested and found to be materials for manufacturing morphine. There is a report form. The case is adjourned again so that various drugs can be studied in detail. The photos of various parts and the two bottles of yellow and black drugs were presented for inspection. After inspecting the various pieces of evidence, the judge ordered a change of date for the trial, and the defendants were still sent back to the police station.

The fifty-first inspection was conducted at the bank on May 29th of the 21st year of the Republic of China, and the Director of the Currency Department of the Ministry of Finance joined the inspection. The inspection results are detailed below. The total amount of exchange voucher issuance is 10,057,2541 yuan, including the bank's issuance of 53,367,850 yuan, the affiliated banks' drawing of 18,882,867 yuan, and the banks and firms' drawing of 28,321,824 yuan. Except for the banks and firms' drawing portion, which will be inspected separately according to the original method, this inspection covers the affiliated bank portion as follows: The bank's issuance and affiliated banks' drawing amount to 72,250,717 yuan. The reserve amount for exchange vouchers of this bank and its affiliated banks is 72,250,717 yuan, including a cash reserve of 43,500,4931.45 yuan and a guarantee reserve of 28,745,785.55 yuan. The above two items, with the cash reserve accounting for 60% and the guarantee reserve accounting for 40%, were all checked and found to be accurate. According to Rule 5, this is a formal report. Chrysler Motors President Moss Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday 173

Mr. Moss, Export President of Chrysler Motors Company of the United States, recently came to the Far East to inspect the automobile business. He arrived in Shanghai yesterday aboard the Dollar Company's President Cleveland. Mr. Flemen, Manager of China Motors Company, and Mr. Madi, Manager of Madi Motors Company, Chrysler's Shanghai agent, hosted a reception for Mr. Moss last night at the Astor House Hotel, inviting members of the Shanghai press and automobile dealers as guests. Eighteen people attended. Chairman Flemen introduced Mr. Moss, who said in his address that he was very pleased to meet everyone. Chrysler is one of the most famous automobile manufacturers in the United States. Its magnificent buildings, with millions of dollars used to build a huge building, are well known to everyone present. Its products, such as Plymouth (Shunfeng brand), Chrysler, etc., are famous all over the world. Recently, the adoption of "floating power" construction has made it even more advanced. This is also a kind of innovation in the automobile industry. Automobiles are very important to human life. In the United States, there are currently no less than 30,000,000 cars. This is true all over the world. Human life can hardly be without this item. My impression of this trip is very deep, and I feel that the beginning of progress has already begun. However, to make it bigger and better, it depends on everyone present. I believe that the most important things in China right now are three things: education, publishing, and transportation. Why? Education enlightens the people, publishing promotes culture, and transportation develops industry. Now those present are newspaper reporters and automobile merchants. This is just my humble opinion, which can be corrected by those with greater knowledge. Mr. Moss finally said that all undertakings based on honesty can succeed. The audience was moved. The reception was accompanied by music and dance, and the guests and hosts parted happily. The humorous remarks of the host, Mr. Flemen, also made those present laugh endlessly.

Foreign Soldiers Rape Female Worker 174

Rickshaw Driver Deserves Praise

Qian Fengying, a 17-year-old woman from Pudong, lives in a bungalow on Gordon Road in western Shanghai and works as a worker in the Hongyu Yarn Factory on Macgregor Road. When they arrived at their destination, five or six foreign soldiers stationed in house number seven next to Zhimin Elementary School dragged her into the room and forcibly raped her until about 4:00 AM yesterday morning. He angrily reported it to the nearby police, who relayed it to the Gordon Road police station. The police sent the woman to the hospital for treatment and notified the commanding officer of the foreign soldiers. The outcome is unknown.

Declaration of the Rent Reduction Committee of Chengde Lane, Guoging Road 181

The declaration of the Rent Reduction Committee of Chengde Lane, Guoging Road states: It is known that during the recent Shanghai Incident, our Guoging Road was also within the fire zone. Although the houses in Chengde Lane were not turned into scorched earth, the residents had all fled. The direct and indirect losses are beyond description. Moreover, the incident happened suddenly, and it was lucky to escape alone. Clothing and goods must not have been moved. Because the junction of the Chinese and French concessions was closed, and traffic was blocked, it was like a prison. Airplanes dropped bombs and set fires, turning the area into rubble. The residents of Guoging Road and its vicinity, supporting the old and carrying the young, rushed to cross the river. Some fell into the river, and some were scattered, causing cries to shake the sky. Any property was abandoned at home, and later suffered from theft by traitors, leaving most families empty. The chaos was such that the vitality was exhausted and there were no tears to cry. It was a catastrophe unprecedented in history. Now that the peace conference has been concluded and the situation is gradually stable, the tenants are gradually moving back. The houses in Chengde Lane on Guoging Road are adjacent to the concessions, so the rents are extraordinarily high. The tenants are mostly poor people. Before the war, it was already difficult to pay the rent. Now, after the war, how can they afford the high rent? Therefore, we have gathered all the tenants in the lane to form a rent reduction committee, with the aim of regulating finance and reducing the burden. We cite the precedents of the capital Zhenjiang, Suzhou, Hangzhou, and the concessions, and make legitimate demands. All tenants, please wait for the authorities to provide fair relief. "Even if the seas run dry and the rocks crumble, this determination will not change." This is our declaration, and we hope for your public understanding.

Famous Doctor Liu Zuotong Relocates Clinic 187

Famous doctor Liu Zuotong (style name Zuotong), specializing in throat and surgical departments, has served as the chief physician of the Guangyi Chinese Medicine Hospital in Nanshi, a professor at the Chinese Medicine College, and a surgical medicine consultant for the local supplement of the News. He also established his own clinic on Fuyou Road, Lao Beimen. Those who came from afar, attracted by his reputation, jostled each other. He has insight into the crux of difficult and complicated diseases. His medical skills are exquisite and miraculous. It is now heard that Mr. Liu has relocated to No. 20 Zhenping Lane, Kaizi'er Road, Songshan Road, French Concession, on the 30th of this month for the convenience of patients' transportation, and will continue to practice medicine as usual.

Letter

To the Editor: In the "Local News" column of your newspaper on the 29th of this month, there was a report that our bureau's "Shangjiang Wheel Emei, while traveling to Fengdu, crashed into a reef due to the captain's negligence. The bow of the ship was immediately broken, and the river water rushed into the front cabin, resulting in the front wheel sinking and the rear rising, which was quite dangerous. Fortunately, the captain urgently ordered the hole to be temporarily repaired, and the ship began to float on the river surface. The goods damaged by water are being checked." After investigation, our bureau's Emei Wheel passed through the Fengdu area, and was two or three miles away from the reef. The bottom of the ship was not broken, and the goods were not damaged by water. What was reported was probably hearsay. We are writing to inform you of this, and we hope you will investigate and correct it. Sincerely, Li Guojie, General Manager of China Merchants Bureau, May 30th.

The Garbage Problem and Shanghai Municipality 190

Compiled by the Cleansing Division of the Shanghai Municipal Health Bureau

The garbage problem arises with the population. Therefore, only large cities have this problem. Shanghai has a population of three million, and garbage has also become a major problem. To solve it is not easy. First, let's describe the methods of large European and American cities, and then discuss the solutions for this city. (1) Methods of disposal of garbage in European and American countries. Regarding the disposal of garbage, all major cities regard it as the most difficult event. Efforts and money are spent, but a thorough solution has not been achieved. European and American cities have spared no effort in research for decades, using machinery or chemistry, but they have never been satisfied. On average, each person discards about half a kilogram (about one pound) of waste every day. The more prosperous the city population, the more garbage is produced. Less is easy to dispose of, more is difficult to manage. For example, Shanghai has a population of three million, which means about 1,500 tons to 2,000 tons of garbage every day. Therefore, sweeping, collecting, transporting, and disposing of it cannot be adequately handled by a small number of people and a small amount of funds. (1) There are two methods for handling sweeping: (A) The local administrative agency handles it themselves, such as the method adopted by the Shanghai authorities. (B) The contractor system. (2) The methods for handling collection are no more than two: mixed collection and classified collection, which are determined by the method of disposal. (3) The method of transportation is either by vehicle or by boat, either self-operated or contracted. However, there are specially equipped vehicles and boats, with the aim of tightly packing and transporting to reduce the leakage of odors and debris. (4) There are many disposal methods, all of which are still in the testing period. Briefly describe them as follows: (A) Reduction. Using chemical methods, the useful oil in the pre-selected garbage is extracted, and the remaining can be used as fertilizer. (B) Incineration. The garbage is first selected and then burned in an incinerator. (C) Fermentation. The garbage must first be selected, and the fermentable animal and plant substances are placed in cement boxes to allow them to ferment and rot. The new product can be used as fertilizer. (D) Feeding. The edible parts are selected for feeding pigs. (E) Filling. Filling low-lying areas and dead canals, using waste to kill two birds with one stone. (F) Dumping on Land. Selecting a remote area in the city to dump and stockpile garbage. (G) Dumpug into Sea. Coastal cities can use ships to transport the garbage several miles outside the harbor and dump it into the sea. (H) Bural. Digging pits and pouring in garbage, covering it with soil. (I) Semerage. The pre-selected garbage is crushed into a slurry and mixed into the sewer for simultaneous disposal in the factory. The above methods have their advantages and disadvantages. Dumping is the most economical, but a single method cannot completely solve the disposal problem. At least one or two methods must assist each other to have hope of a solution. (2) Garbage situation in Shanghai. The garbage in Shanghai is collected in three places. The situation is listed below.

Shanghai Municipal Government Directly Under its Jurisdiction Public Concession French Concession

Population 1.88 million (January) 1 million 430,000

(Including only 850,000 in the city, the garbage produced is transported by ship. The garbage from the remaining rural areas is filled locally.)

Approximate amount of garbage 600 tons (daily) 1,000 tons (daily) 500 tons (daily)

Cleaning method Managed by the Health Bureau Managed by the Public Works Department Managed by the Engineering Department

Number of cleaners 524 1,300 308

Collection method Wooden carts, automobiles (mixed collection) Wooden carts, automobiles, horse-drawn carts (mixed collection) Horse-drawn carts, automobiles (mixed collection)

Transportation method Contractor system (Fan Lushun) Contractor system (Gu Chunji) Contractor system (Gu Yunji)

Automobile Barge Automobile Barge Barge

Transportation cost 3,750 yuan (monthly) 14,850 taels (monthly) 5,000 taels (monthly)

Disposal method Filling (100 tons) Incineration (300 tons) Dumping (500 tons)

Dumping (500 tons) Dumping (700 tons)

Financial: Yesterday's Gold Bar Fluctuations Trended Higher, Rebounding Three Taels and Two Mace 191

A Strong Downward Trend Was Observed the Day Before Yesterday

A Swing of Six Taels and a Half: Yesterday, the 31st, the gold bar market showed signs of a rebound, rising again. Although there were no drastic changes, there was a swing of six taels and a half throughout the day. Ultimately, it rebounded three taels and some odd change. With no trading in American silver, larger bars rose slightly, and the intentions of fellow traders remained firm, leading to a prompt price increase. Subsequently, there were favorable factors such as the British exchange rate easing and the American exchange rate holding firm. However, the cashiers of various firms varied in their practices, resulting in occasional fluctuations. The market trend seemed to weaken later, and the exchange rate eased slightly, hence the rise of three or four taels. Finally, it settled at 771.2 taels. Today (June 1st) is the time when the money industry closes its books at the end of May and takes a holiday, resulting in a city-wide market closure for one day. Detailed market conditions before and after are listed below:

The Morning Market Was Promising: From the opening at 7 AM, prices immediately rose by one tael, reaching 712.5 taels. The British silver rate remained unchanged in the near term and rose one-sixteenth in the long term. There was no market for silver prices, but buyers were active, and the opening price was high. Heng Yuanyuan, Heng Tai Chang, Yi Feng, and Yong Jun advanced. They then raised the price by more than two taels to fifteen taels. Yu He and Yuan Mao Yong Lai sold, immediately dropping one tael to thirteen taels and eight mace. However, British gold was absorbed by Mitsui at 1.79375 for July, and Citibank bought 31.375 for August. Zhifeng, Yong Qian, and Chang Xiang, among others, bought, immediately adding 2.9 taels at a quarter past the hour to reach 15.8 taels. However, British gold for June was available for purchase at 0.9375. Furthermore, there seemed to be more buyers than sellers of American gold for June at 0.625, which led to a decrease to 14 taels. The announcement of British gold remaining unchanged and American gold decreasing by 0.25, along with internal strengthening, with American gold for June trading at 30.05, especially with the eager purchases from Xie Xing Yong, Heng Xing Yuan, Hong Li, Heng Yu, Da De Cheng, Zhi Feng Yong, among others, caused the price to leap by more than two taels to 16.5 taels at 10:00 AM. Soon after, Yi Feng Yong, Bing Xing, Tong Tai Chang, Yuan Mao Yong, Yuan Yuan, Kang Xiang, Hong Kang, and Yong, among others, all sold. Furthermore, HSBC issued British gold for June and July at 8 pence, while American gold for September was available for sale at 31.6875 yuan. As a result, gold prices deteriorated, falling by five taels to 11.5 taels at 10:30 AM. After that, Yi Feng Yong, Da De Cheng, Yu He, and Fu Chang, among others, bought, raising it again to 14.2 taels. After 10:45 AM, Wan Xing Shun Li and retail investors came to sell, causing it to drop again by more than one tael to 12.7 taels at 11:00 AM, partly because Hua Bi absorbed British gold for July at 0.625 and American gold absorbed at 8 pence. With more buyers appearing on the surface, the price immediately surged by 2 taels to 14.5 taels after 11:30 AM. However, Heng Yu and others disposed of套頭物品 again, bringing it back to 13.2 taels. The noon closing price was 13.8 taels, and the announced price changed to 800 taels, with a discount of 85 to 86 taels to a noon closing of 86 taels.

The Afternoon Market Turned Weak: The afternoon market opened at 13.6 taels. Yi Feng then entered the market and bought British gold for August at 0.0625 and American gold for October at 31.875 yuan, absorbing it steadily. By around 2:30 PM, it was 14.4 taels. However, sellers did not slacken, with Zhi Feng Yong, Heng Yu, Hong Kang Yong, Bing Xing, and Yuan Mao Yong, among others, disposing of their holdings, especially due to the loose exchange market. Mitsui issued American gold for September at 31.75 yuan and British gold for June at 0.0625, seemingly requiring 1.875 to be sold in September, which led to a softening of the market. The price fell by more than four taels, to 10 taels at 3:00 PM (the lowest price of the day). Afterwards, Yi Feng and others bought again, bringing it to 13.5 taels at 3:40 PM. Fu Xing Yong and others sold, and British gold for August could be settled at 1.25, bringing it to 11.2 taels at 4:00 PM. General retail short sellers came to cover their positions, because today (June 1st) is a holiday and they needed to balance their accounts. As a result, it rebounded by two taels to 13.2 taels. By the closing at 4:30 PM, it was 12.7 taels, a rebound of 3.2 taels compared to the day before yesterday. However, Zhi Feng Yong and others sold again, falling back to slightly over 11 taels. The highest price of the day was 16.5 taels, and the lowest was 10 taels, a difference of 6.5 taels. The announced discount ranged from 90 taels to 87-88 taels. The recorded price was 14 taels, with a supplementary payment of 14 taels. The net red strip for the afternoon was calculated at 13 taels plus 8 taels and 7.5 mace.

Supplementary Record of Market Conditions the Day Before Yesterday (May 30th): The gold exchange continued to operate as usual on May 30th. American Cotton Prices Trended Lower Last Week 200

There Is a Theory of Selling Stored Cotton in the South

New York, May 27th telegram, announcing the cotton market situation for the week, says: The spot cotton market has been uneven this week, and prices have a tendency to loosen, because the climate is suitable, and cotton crop development is relatively good. Also, because the tax problem is uncertain, and the trade report has not improved. Southern cotton factories, due to the accumulation of stored cotton or inventory, have slightly sold short, and the bulls have also slightly closed out, so New York has slightly risen in selling. The spot market situation in the South has not been weak, and the number of sales is still small. When the spot goods fall slightly, the shorts and fellow traders buy in, so they can maintain the popularity in the spot goods market. However, buyers would rather wait for others to sell than to seek to buy themselves. In several places in the cotton belt, the night temperature is quite low, and the rainfall is also excessive, resulting in the saying that cotton crop progress is slow. Some people also say that there is a need to replant, but the dry land in the eastern part of the cotton belt has seen rain, and the soil moisture is quite good.

Silk, Tea, Jiangning Cocoon Market Desolate 204

Few Cocoon Businesses, Small Cocoon Prices

Most Silkworm Farmers Self-Bake

In the towns and villages of Jiangning, many farmers now raise foreign seeds from the Breeding Improvement Association, so although the cocoon production is scarce, the cocoon quality is still good. However, no one has rented the cocoon businesses in the four villages, and only one in the urban area weighs and receives cocoons, and receives cocoons at a limited price. The highest price for high-quality cocoons is only 20 to 25 yuan, and the lowest is only 15 yuan. The silkworm farmers' losses are too great, and most use the native method to bake them in preparation for spinning native silk themselves. The cocoon market is desolate this time, and the impact on farmers and silkworms is extraordinary.

Free Talk

The Sayings of Old Man Ma Xiangbo, Ninety-Three

Is it Better to Compliment Students or Teachers? 212

—

When I was in Japan, I was very unconvinced about Japan. One day, our embassy held a grand banquet. Diplomats from various countries and prominent Japanese figures attended. It was lively and bustling. As a counselor, everyone asked me to say a few words. I thought diplomatic rhetoric should not offend people. So, I stood up and said:

"Not long ago, I traveled in Europe and saw the European political stage, which was truly colorful and fascinating. European politics is indeed more enlightened than that of the East. European society is indeed more advanced than that of the East. I couldn't help but admire what I saw!

"Now that I come to the East, I suddenly see a large mirror on this Eastern political stage that reflects the things on the Western stage exactly, vividly. I am even more surprised!

"It's like a student imitating a teacher, surpassing the teacher. If the teacher is good, the student is not bad either. Should I compliment the student or the teacher? I really feel a bit hesitant."

The applause was like thunder. Many foreigners in the diplomatic corps specifically came forward to shake my hand and congratulate me. The Japanese guests could not help but smile and nod.

Reversing the Tide of January 29th 213

— Yu Jianhua

The Shanghai battle has lasted more than a month. A kind of Liu Bowen stele was suddenly discovered on the streets. It spoke of this incident as being in accordance with its predictions. Newspaper vendors seized the opportunity to reprint it, and it became popular for a while. Everything it said had already been fulfilled. Only the last two lines, "Reversing the tide on January 29th, witnessing the sun set in the West," have not yet been precisely identified. However, although the Shanghai Incident is said to have started on January 28th, it actually started late at night. The actual contact, however, was on January 29th. Moreover, the troops resisting Japan alone happened to be the 19th Route Army. Many people say that the 19th Route Army's uprising on January 29th was an opportunity for China to be reborn, enough to reverse the will of Heaven. By the time the National Army retreated to the second line of defense due to lack of support, the nation's passionate hope dissolved like ice and snow. Then, on April 29th, just when the Japanese army was elated, there was a sudden loud noise. Yin Bong-gil's bomb wiped out Japanese army dignitaries, causing numerous deaths and injuries. Currently, our country is holding a memorial service for the fallen soldiers in Suzhou, bringing matters to a close. Shirakawa has already died from his injuries and his body has been transported back to his country. The day of his arrival in the country also happened to be May 29th. The beginning and end of the war are both inseparable from the number 29. Is there then a fate related to this number? However, victory or defeat depends on making every effort. One should not rely solely on fate to comfort oneself, suppress one's fighting spirit, and hinder one's progress.

The Nation is Beyond Saving 214

— Sun Guliang

Someone said, "The nation is in such a dire situation, with national demise imminent. Yet you say the nation is beyond saving. Are you not insane?" I said, "Yes, yes, no, no. If one could follow even one of my proposed five methods, the nation would indeed be beyond saving! The methods are simple, and the implementation is easy, but they are not known to you and are not what the virtuous and talented of the party-state like to hear. What are these methods? It is the transformation of the heart! Please allow me to explain my methods":

(1) To use the heart of civil war, full of bravery, against foreign enemies will render the nation beyond saving.

(2) To use the heart of deceiving the people, full of cunning, in diplomacy will render the nation beyond saving.

(3) To use the heart of non-resistance, full of cowardice, in civil war will render the nation beyond saving.

(4) To use the heart of plundering, full of selfish desires, in national defense will render the nation beyond saving.

(5) To use the heart of diplomacy, full of gentleness, in uniting the people will render the nation beyond saving.

That person clapped his hands with tears in his eyes and retreated.

Movies with a Common Touch 215

— Cangshi

Recently, the domestic film industry has been following almost the same path, which is love movies. Zhang San loves Li Si, and Li Si reforms. It's all the same, and it's getting a little annoying. Sometimes there are some different plots, but most of them are descriptions of the aristocratic class. Film art has simply become entertainment for young masters and misses. Tianyi Company's new sound film "A Married Woman" depicts a poor working-class couple who suffer from the pressures of making a living. The wife is also seduced by a wealthy young man, eventually falling from grace. As a result, both the worker and the wealthy young man are tragically killed. The plot is very intense and exciting, and the actors are well-chosen (starring Xuan Jinglin, Sun Min, Zhang Zhenduo, and Li Lilian). Their expressions are realistic, adding many touching elements.

Yesterday, the film was previewed at the New Light Grand Theater. After watching it, I was very moved. I felt that the plot of the film completely broke away from the usual nauseating love stories. It tasted different. In this era, this kind of film that speaks for the common people is very valuable. I think enthusiastic friends will definitely sympathize with this poor "Married Woman," right?

World News in Brief 216

— Haike

A Wonderful Painting Reunited – About five hundred years ago, there was an unknown French painter who painted a wonderful painting of the Great Flood from ancient times. This painting was very, very large and painted with great detail. After it was finished, it was cut into four pieces. But each piece could stand alone and become a very good painting. After many years, these four pieces of painting were scattered. One piece was displayed in the Louvre Museum in Paris, France. The whereabouts of the other three pieces were unknown. Later, after much effort, it was discovered that the second piece was in Amsterdam, the capital of the Netherlands, the third piece was in Brussels, the capital of Belgium, and the fourth piece was in England and was privately owned. Each of these four pieces of painting had a photograph. When put together, they were indeed a complete painting. Two years ago, an exhibition was held in Paris, where these four pieces of painting were brought together. It was truly a rare masterpiece. Recently, a French painting exhibition was held in London, where this painting, reunited after being separated, was displayed again for the public to enjoy.

Aspects of Life in Soviet Russia (Continued) 217

— Mo Yi

A foreigner once criticized, "Russia is a place where there is always happiness and people can meet with happiness everywhere. If a Russian can get a piece of white bread, or three yards of coarse cloth, or a pair of socks, this will be the seed of his happiness." People like us who have tightened to the extreme, without food when hungry and without clothes when cold, feel happy when we get every small object, so we think his words are correct.

Today I did something very happy. I bought a pair of rubber shoes for twelve rubles. (They used to cost only one ruble and twenty kopecks.) But first I had to hand over three pairs of old shoes and pre-write a receipt, and when I picked up the shoes, I used this receipt and twelve rubles to exchange for them. Now it's spring, and the weather is humid. We certainly have to protect the hygiene of our feet, so I bought a pair for the price of twelve rubles. To be honest, our only industry now is health. Besides that, everything else has been seized by the government. But then again, I always feel that it is much better than the workers in capitalist countries, working with empty stomachs in the iron grip of capitalists. In other words, we will not lose our jobs or go hungry, even though we are so painful.

The most interesting thing in Moscow is a kind of aristocratic joint store with the words "This store only accepts cash or foreign currency" written at the door. This is written in Russian. Foreigners who don't know Russian will of course not understand, so there is a doorman who whispers to customers when they enter the door, "Only gold or foreign currency." This method of collecting cash from the people often stirs people's emotions and makes them uneasy. And these stores sell daily necessities, so there are some people who really have no other way but to take their last wedding gold ring or gold cross and exchange it for a shirt, a pair of shoes, or a bedspread, etc. The price is extremely high. Shoes that cost one hundred and seventy rubles elsewhere can be sold for three or four foreign dollars in these stores. What we get as salary is paper money, but when we buy things, we know we have to pay cash or foreign currency. Do you think there is any other country's people besides the Russian people who can endure this? We are all forced to work desperately, dumping the goods we have worked hard to create to foreign countries, so that the country can collect as much cash as possible from foreign countries and concentrate it in Russia, which excites people with revolutions around the world. What benefits do we people know about?

Random Notes on the Memorial Service for the Fallen Soldiers in the Battle of Shanghai 218

— Cheng Xiaoqing

The Grand and Solemn Venue On May 28th, the weather was slightly overcast, neither hot nor cold; it was as if Heaven also deliberately showed its dim and sorrowful face to mourn the anti-Japanese generals and soldiers who sacrificed their heads and shed their blood for the country's survival and the nation's glory. The venue was the Wang Feiji Public Sports Field in the city. In front of the gate and on the altar in the center, there were white and blue memorial arches, tall and magnificent, which truly represented the personalities and spirits of the martyrs. Around the venue, Boy Scouts and military police were strictly stationed. There were three entrances and exits to the venue, and the entry and exit of the public groups and the army were not mixed, and the order was well maintained. The preparatory committee pre-made various badges. Only those who wore badges were allowed to enter the venue. Only those who wore yellow badges were allowed to go directly to the altar. The memorial service was scheduled to begin at ten o'clock, but by nine o'clock, representatives from all over the country and various organizations in the city, American expatriates, etc., had almost filled the venue; and the public without badges, surrounded outside the venue, numbered no less than 30,000 to 50,000 people. What a grand occasion! The presidium consisted of Chen Mingshu, Dai Ji, Cai Tingkai, Jiang Guangnai, and Zhang Zhizhong. The chief officiant was Ju Zheng, and the general commander of the venue was Weng Zhaoyuan, who steadfastly defended Wusong. Unfortunately, the reporter was far away from the altar, and the faces of the dignitaries could not be seen clearly, and the speeches could not be heard either.

The Dense Couplets and Elegiac Scrolls Around the venue, bamboo racks were pre-erected, covered with elegiac scrolls, the number of which was countless. If they were connected end to end and stretched, they could reach the station directly. The witty remarks in the couplets were also endless. If they could be compiled and published, it would be of permanent commemorative value. A couplet by Zhang Junsong, the head of the 156th Brigade at the main entrance, was magnificent and worth reciting, and is specially recorded as follows: "They are the pillars of the country and the vanguards of the nation, swallowing the Dwarf bandits, and their divine bravery far shakes the whole world!" "Sacrificing for justice and fighting for peace, their blood splashed on the Shanghai wilderness, and their loyal souls will forever surround the Great Jiangnan!" Other silver shields and wreaths piled up. In addition to sending more than 300 yuan in condolences, our Soochow University also joined other church schools to send a large silver shield, engraved with the twelve characters "The blood of the martyrs, the soul of the Chinese nation, lasts forever, and their noble spirit exists!" As for the propaganda printed matter, it was flying everywhere, and there were various kinds. The preparatory committee produced a memorial publication, which listed the names and resumes of the dead and wounded officers and soldiers in great detail. Unfortunately, the reporter followed the Soochow University team from the side door and could not obtain it. I borrowed it once and recorded the casualty table on the left:

Casualties of Officers and Soldiers in the Anti-Japanese War of the 19th Army and the 5th Army

Wounded in battle Dead in battle Remarks

Unit Rank and file Soldiers Rank and file Soldiers

61st Division 195 2802 46 843

Respectable and Lovely Glorious Warriors On that day, about three regiments of soldiers from the 19th Army and about one regiment from the 5th Army participated. The officers and soldiers of the 5th Army wore yellow woolen uniforms, neat and solemn, with robust bodies and full spirits; the 19th Army wore blue-grey cloth uniforms, short pants exposing their knees, and wore the glorious and supreme 19th Route Army battle hats, which were admired by foreigners (it is said that this battle hat has been carried by Americans to their country and placed in the museum). Although their stature was shorter, they were brave and lively, which truly represented the national soul of our Chinese nation. As the reporter passed by them, his blood boiled and his spirit moved. He not only changed the past psychology of hating soldiers because of hating civil wars, but also wanted to pay homage to these sacred warriors who defended the country and loved the people! A Tragic and Passionate Atmosphere In addition to being filled with a solemn and tragic atmosphere, the venue had a gratifying phenomenon. That is, 99% of the men and women participating in the memorial service in the entire venue, whether in uniforms or casual clothes, were wearing domestic cloth and silk. Occasionally, one or two so-called modern men and women who usually wear imported goods to show off their beauty were overshadowed at this time and felt ashamed. The reporter believes that if this phenomenon can be popularized outside the venue and continue permanently, it will be the only panacea to save our dying national destiny! This is the responsibility that all of our people should fulfill, and it is easy to do if we are determined. If we cannot sacrifice and eliminate the psychology of admiring foreign goods, then how can we face the fallen generals and soldiers who donated their lives and abandoned their homes? I now respectfully ask the gentlemen of the government, the leaders of society, and the educated young students to take the lead in advocating this only panacea for resurrection!

Contributions of Personal Feelings Alas! The dead are gone! What contributions will those who die later make? The lost land in the Northeast has not been recovered, and what will be the reliance of the martyrs' families? I heard from a certain soldier who participated in the war that the government's treasury is exhausted, and the pensions for the fallen generals and soldiers have not been issued to this day. The martyrs regarded death as going home and died in the right place; however, their widows and orphans, and their elderly parents, have lost their support. How will they make a living? To put it simply, our lives and property have been preserved by the blood of the soldiers, and we should not indifferently forget these widows and orphans without thinking of how to repay them? As the reporter puts pen to paper, he wishes to dedicate his sincerity to encourage all his compatriots! (Please ask the Shenbao Accounting Office to transfer this manuscript's remuneration to the Weiguo Warriors Family Support Association)

Local Supplement of Shenbao

Sayings

Women Smoking and Morality 219

— Songlu

According to the Tokyo dispatch of the World Society yesterday, the government's tobacco monopoly bureau recently announced the sale of a new type of cigarette specifically for women, which has aroused great opposition from the female community. Various women's groups have sent representatives to visit the bureau chief, saying that this move is tantamount to the government encouraging women to smoke, hindering social morality, and demanding the cancellation of the new cigarette sales plan.

Whether women smoking is related to morality is indeed an interesting question worth studying. Originally, cigarettes are harmful and useless, which no one can deny. What we want to study now are two questions: one is whether women can smoke, and the other is whether women smoking is related to morality.

Regarding whether women can smoke, I think it is absolutely possible, because according to the principle of equality between men and women, if men can smoke, why can't women? Regarding morality, according to this principle, it is the same. If men smoking has nothing to do with morality, how can women smoking be related to morality? Could it be that bad morality can only be promoted by men, and women cannot emulate it?

This article is originally about Japanese affairs, which is not related to us, and we don't need to speak for the Japanese authorities. However, the trend of women smoking cigarettes in our country is probably more serious than in Japan. From aristocratic ladies to common women, they all have the idea of "a cigarette after a meal is like living a god." Although women smoking cigarettes is not prohibited by law, it still creates a non-benevolent habit. From a moral point of view, it is always better to try to eliminate it. Originally, women's consumables are already too many. If we really talk about the reason for equal consumption, it is not an exaggeration to not allow women to smoke, because they consume more than men in makeup and clothing. Let's leave the smoking matter to men's "patent."

However, from a proper principle, not only should women smoking be opposed, but also men smoking should not be allowed. It is really "laborious and costly" and results in no benefits at all, but is harmful to health. Why bother?

Responding to Meng Shao'an's Feelings After the Enemy's Retreat, Original Rhymes 220

— Chen Baoren

Half of the southeast has been washed by war, enduring to see the old mountains and rivers. After the battlefield war, there are remnants of hills, lamenting the passing waves of the sea. Dejected, the insects and sand lament the great calamity, and the desolate home is full of tears. The most heartbreaking is the Wusong willow, quietly standing in the east wind, calling what to do.

Same as Above 221

— Gu Zuliang

When the peace agreement was reached, the weapons were laid down together, but the broken ruins were no longer the old mountains and rivers. The enemy cavalry retreated, leaving behind traces of destruction. Pleasure boats return, mourning the green waves. The battlefield is desolate with few people, and the concessions are prosperous with many pipes. Even if one survives after the calamity, what about the unhealed wounds?

Science

Glycerin 222

— Commoner

Glycerin has extremely wide uses in industry. Here, its properties, manufacturing methods, and uses are described separately as follows:

Glycerin is a colorless, viscous liquid with a sweet taste. In Western languages, it is called Glycerin. Its molecular formula is C3H8O3. It belongs to the trihydric alcohol group in organic substances. In its pure state, it crystallizes at 17 degrees Celsius and boils at 290 degrees Celsius. The human body contains a small amount in the blood. Lecithin and fat in the brain are both compounds of glycerin. Industrially, various vegetable oils and fats are used, and methods are devised to decompose them into fatty acids and glycerin. Fatty acids are the main raw material for making candles. Sodium and potassium salts of fatty acids are soap. Therefore, the by-products of candle factories and soap factories become the major source of glycerin.

There are various methods for obtaining glycerin from animal and vegetable oils and fats: (1) Adding clean water and a small amount of catalyst, such as lime or zinc oxide, to the fat. These can all be used as catalysts for decomposing oils and fats. Then, heating this mixture under high pressure of six to eight times atmospheric pressure to 170 degrees Celsius, the oils and fats decompose into fatty acids and glycerin. (2) Adding a type of yeast to the water-containing mixture of oils and fats. This yeast is usually extracted from castor seeds. Then, adding a small amount of acid to make it slightly acidic, and heating to 40 degrees Celsius, the oils and fats will spontaneously decompose. (3) Adding concentrated sulfuric acid or caustic soda, or caustic potash, to the oils and fats, and then heating and boiling it, glycerin can also decompose freely. This method was commonly used by candle factories and soap factories in the past. (4) Recently, some people have used sulfonic acid and sulfonic acid derivatives as catalysts, adding them to the oils and fats, and then adding a small amount of clean water, heating to 100 degrees Celsius, glycerin will spontaneously precipitate out. According to the first and fourth methods, the glycerin obtained is very pure, which is the new method that is currently popular. During the European War, the glycerin needed by the Germans was used for manufacturing explosives. The supply could not meet the demand. The German, Constan, greatly improved the yeast in the second method. First, he used starch to make sugar, and then added an equal amount of sodium sulfite and yeast to the sugar to ferment it. This could reduce the production of alcohol from 40 percent to 23 percent, and increase the production of glycerin from 11 percent to 27 percent. Unfortunately, the cost of this method was too high, losing its market competitiveness, and it is still not used by industrialists.

The biggest use of glycerin in industry is for making explosives. The famous Dynamite is made by absorbing nitrated glycerin into fine sand powder. For its manufacturing method, please refer to this column of this newspaper on the 13th of this month. In addition, cosmetics, such as lipstick, hair gel, hair oil, mouthwash, toothpaste, etc., used by women, all contain it. In medicine, it can be made into ointments and used in winter to prevent skin from freezing and cracking, as well as for moisturizing the skin. It is also not easy to dry out. When mixed with rosin, sesame oil, beeswax, etc., it can be made into indoor mosquito-catching glue. When mixed with formalin, it can be used to kill insects in orchards. Other things like typewriter ribbons, carbon paper, stamp pads, printing ink, etc., are all mixtures of glycerin and color pigments. Glycerin liquid has elasticity, so recoil mechanisms for guns and hydraulic machines also use it. If glycerin is mixed with potassium soap solution and turpentine to wipe glass windows, water vapor will not condense on them in winter and obstruct visibility. Therefore, aviators must first wipe their glasses with glycerin soap before flying. It is also used for glazing cotton yarn, preventing water in gas meters from freezing, and blending various food and wine flavors. Finally, glycerin mixed with lead oxide powder is the best adhesive for metal, stone, and glass.

Learning

Foreign Son-in-Law 223

— Zewei

The principal of F Middle School is a person who greatly admires Westernization. He is particularly proficient in English, so he specially hired a young American female teacher to teach the English course for Class A of the second year of junior high school. This female teacher is very young, only about twenty years old. She especially likes to dress up in colorful clothes. Every time she comes to the classroom to teach, the classroom is immediately filled with an incredible fragrance, almost anesthetizing the whole body.

Mister K is the best in English in his grade. None of the students in the whole grade can compare with him. When it comes to conversation, he is truly fluent and familiar with the subject matter. Therefore, the young female teacher likes him very much.

K's seat is in the front row, very close to the podium. One day, it was English class again. Other students hate English very much, but K is always delighted whenever it is English class. Before the class bell even rang, K was already sitting at his desk.

"Ding-ling! Ding-ling! Ding-ling! : : :"

The class bell rang, and the students gradually walked into the classroom from outside. The young female teacher, holding a foreign book, also walked in afterward.

"Old K, today is your lucky day again. Even I am benefiting from that fragrant scent!" T, who was sitting in the row behind K, gently kicked K's chair as he said this.

"You smooth-talker," K said with a smile and scolding tone.

After taking attendance, the female teacher taught a lesson and then smiled and pointed at K to explain a passage. K listened as if he had received an imperial decree, and quickly stood up, holding the book and began to explain it with a murmur. The female teacher walked off the podium and sat on K's desk, listening to his explanation. T, who was behind K, was already intoxicated.

After K finished explaining the book, the female teacher put down the book, pointed to a word with her right finger, while stroking K's hair, and said in the local language.

"You mispronounced this word. It should be read with a high tone, but you read it with a low tone." As she spoke, her head was almost leaning against K's head.

At this time, K had no mind to listen to her explanation at all, and was already anesthetized and his whole body was weak.

The bell for the end of class interrupted K's opportunity to enjoy his good fortune. Many students rushed out of the classroom before the teacher could leave. The young female teacher also left gracefully with her book. T, D, and S, who were next to K, came over with giggles. D said: "K, congratulations, that Miss is in love with you!"

"Don't talk nonsense," K said, "Did you see it?" "Oh my! The foreign son-in-law has a big attitude," S said, clapping his hands.

K suddenly stood up and ran out of the classroom. So, many students kept shouting, "Foreign son-in-law!"

Nonsense

A and B 224

— I

A: I heard that you have been frequently publishing some "literary" "small talks" in newspapers recently. Is that true?

B: Yes, yes, and sometimes I "casually talk" about "science" too. But they are all "nonsensical" things, and I still need Mr. Qing to give me some guidance. A: Easy, easy! Like your previous book "Tan Ying," it is enough of a warning to those who "live in a drunken dream." But, "alas! The state of the world is declining, what is the use of talking!" B: Yes. There is really no way to help those who are "beyond help." But articles like "School Scene Snapshots," I think, at least have some remedial effect for students, right?

A: That's certainly true. For example, there are many "unimaginable" things in "streets and alleys." Logically, we should "expose their tricks" and see if they are "ashamed" or not?

B: Exactly, even if it is just "a scale or a claw," we should "record everything we hear."

A: That's exactly what I mean! As long as it is a problem that occurs in "a corner of society," no matter "east, west, south, or north," even if it is just "bamboo scraps and wood chips," we must analyze it to see "why?" it is like this, and where the root cause lies.

B: Absolutely, absolutely. From national affairs to "market news," everything is worth our attention.

A: However, some people only talk about "movies" or "sexual issues," which is really "inexplicable."

B: That's true, but what can we do for the "bread problem"?

A: So, you yourself are writing articles for a living? That's "utterly absurd."

B: Actually, we are all "without a way out"! You don't have to criticize others.

A: No, you are really "pitiable!"

B: However, you also seem to be very serious, which is also "laughable!"

Market News

Lu Wenzhong's Miraculous Security Water. Lu Wenzhong's Miraculous Security Water, generally distributed by Lianyi Trading Company at No. 474 Nanjing Road, is a secret formula obtained by Mr. Lu. He has been formulating and distributing it for years. It has been incredibly effective in treating epidemics. After more than ten years of treatment effectiveness and research, it is now being made public. At the cost of huge sums of money, it is carefully produced according to the formula. As summer approaches and epidemics gradually arise, charitable people from this city and other ports are ordering it one after another for distribution.

Letter Received: To the Editor, I recently saw a column on chemistry in the Shanghai Zengkan of your newspaper on May 24th, which was on glass etching in chemical art and small industries. The mixture of calcium fluoride and sulfuric acid, which is its main raw material, is extremely poisonous. If it touches the skin, it will cause incurable ulcers. I hope this can be published in the newspaper so that those who try it can be careful. If you are exposed to this substance, wash it off with water within two or three seconds to avoid this danger. Yu Bingshen

▲ Wang Shaoqing petitions for preliminary attachment. Upon investigation, the plaintiff in case No. 259 in the Dizzi Year 20 is Wang Yan. The petitioner in this case is Wang Shaoqing. It must be clarified in a petition whether Wang Shaoqing and Wang Yan are the same person.

▲ Chen Baozhen petitions for completion of the case. Approved for completion of the case.

▲ One item: Xu Liangtian petitions for execution. A hearing has been scheduled for 8:00 AM on June 3rd. You must appear in court on time.

▲ Fan Jingmei requests execution. Upon investigation, the case file has not yet been returned by the Third Branch of the High Court. The request should be postponed for consideration.

▲ Chongxian requests a second sealing. Upon investigation, the movable property of the debtor, Yan Ziliang, was previously sealed by the Public Concession Court, and a auction has been scheduled. The request should be notified and sealed after the auction.

▲ Zhengye Company Leasing Office petitions for closing the case and receiving the funds. Approved for closing the case, and you must come to the court at 2:00 PM on June 6th to receive the funds.

▲ Ma Guijie petitions for execution. Upon investigation, the case file has not yet been returned by the appellate court. The request should be postponed for consideration.

▲ Wei Wenzeng petitions for execution and to receive funds. Upon investigation, the case has been finalized. The 200 yuan provided by the debtor as security during the preliminary attachment should be released first. The petitioner must come to the court at 9:00 AM on June 3rd to receive the funds. As for the remaining debt owed by the debtor, a hearing should be scheduled to execute it.

▲ Yipin Bank petitions for sealing. The case has already been scheduled for sealing. Regarding the claim that the debtor has emptied the furniture, the actual situation should be investigated at the scheduled time and sealed. If the debtor has concealed property, the petitioner should file a private prosecution with the Criminal Division according to the law. (Above: May 31st)

Shanghai Local Court 229

Criminal Judgments: Zhang Zhou Opium Case: Zhang Zhou is fined seventy yuan for possessing opium smoking paraphernalia for criminal use. If the fine is not paid after compulsory enforcement, it shall be commuted to imprisonment at the rate of one yuan per day. The number of days of detention shall be used to offset the fine at the rate of two yuan per day. One opium tray, one small spoon, one pair of opium tongs, and one digging tool; and seven each of opium pipes and lamps, four each of opium tongs and skewers, three digging tools, eight qian of opium ashes, and a small amount of red pills are to be confiscated.

▲ Wang Degui and Others Opium Case: Wang Degui is sentenced to six months imprisonment and fined sixty yuan for providing premises for others to smoke opium. Shen Haishan, Li Hairong, Wu Liansheng, Yu Alai, Lu A’mei, and Cheng Jinglin are each sentenced to one month imprisonment and fined fifteen yuan for smoking opium. If the fine is not paid after compulsory enforcement, it shall be commuted to imprisonment at the rate of one yuan per day. The number of days detained shall be used to offset the imprisonment at the rate of two days for one day of imprisonment. Three opium pipes, three opium lamps, one opium tray, one opium bowl, and one opium box with a small amount of opium ash inside shall be confiscated and burned.

▲ Li Achao and Others Robbery Case: Public prosecution of Li Achao is not accepted. Trial of Wang Tianxi’s part is suspended.

▲ Shi Agen Embezzlement Case: Shi Agen is sentenced to six months imprisonment for embezzling items held in the course of his duties. The number of days detained shall be used to offset the imprisonment at the rate of two days for one day of imprisonment.

▲ Cai Xiaoliuzi Theft Case: Cai Xiaoliuzi is sentenced to one year imprisonment for the crime of theft at the wharf. The number of days detained shall be used to offset the imprisonment at the rate of two days for one day of imprisonment.
